					add_to_variable = { int_investments = BLR.int_investments }
				}
				UKR = {

				add_to_variable = { debt = SOV.debt }
				add_to_variable = { int_investments = SOV.int_investments }
				for_each_loop = {
					array = missile_inventory_array
					value = v
					index = i

					array = GNSS_satellite_array
					value = v

					value = v
					index = i

					}

					value = v
